<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суровый.html>суро́вый</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">suróvyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суровость.html>суро́вость</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">suróvostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суровость.html>суро́вости</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суровость.html>суро́вости</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суровость.html>суро́востей</a></b>)
</p>

<li>sternness</li></ol>

***суровый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:суровый.html>суро́вый</a> (2658)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">суровъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">surovŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суровый.html>суро́вый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">suróvyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)суро́вее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)суро́вей</b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">суро́вейший</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>severe, strict, harsh, stern, austere, rigorous</li>
<li>severe, inclement</li>
<li>stern, inexorable, severe</li>
<li>unbleached, brown (cloth)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строгий.html>стро́гий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">strógij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жесткий.html>жёсткий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">žóstkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:неумолимый.html>неумоли́мый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">neumolímyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***сурок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a> (22312)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Vasmer, there are two possible origins:
</p>
<ol><li>A borrowing from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о́к</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ók</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kazakh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kazakh language">Kazakh</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="kk">суыр</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="kk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">swır</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">marmot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kyrgyz_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kyrgyz language">Kyrgyz</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ky">суур</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ky-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">suur</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">marmot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chuvash_language" class="extiw" title="w:Chuvash language">Chuvash</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="cv">сӑвӑр</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">săvăr</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">marmot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li>
<li>Onomatopoetic, based on its characteristic whistle. In this case, it would be cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sōrex</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shrew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ὕραξ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">húrax</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">shrew</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">स्वरति</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svárati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sound, to ring</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">svara</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sound</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">svišť</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">marmot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">svišť</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">marmot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">świszcz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">marmot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> , cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:свистать.html>свиста́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svistátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to whistle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">surók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>сурка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>сурки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>сурко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>marmot
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:альпийский.html>альпи́йский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">alʹpíjskij <b>surók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">alpine marmot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">байбак</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">bajbak</i> ― <span class="e-translation">bobak marmot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:степной.html>степно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">stepnój <b>surók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">steppe marmot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">ванкуверский <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vankuverskij <b>surók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Vancouver Island marmot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">гимала́йский <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gimalájskij <b>surók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Himalayan marmot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">длиннохвостый <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dlinnoxvostyj <b>surók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">long-tailed marmot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">желтобрю́хий <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">želtobrjúxij <b>surók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">yellow-bellied marmot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:красный.html>кра́сный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krásnyj <b>surók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">red marmot, golden marmot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">лесостепно́й <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lesostepnój <b>surók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">forest-steppe marmot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лесной.html>лесно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b>, североамерика́нский <a href = vnd.unilang:лесной.html>лесно́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lesnój <b>surók</b>, severoamerikánskij lesnój <b>surók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">groundhog, woodchuck</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:монгольский.html>монго́льский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">mongólʹskij <b>surók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Mongolian marmot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:олимпийский.html>олимпи́йский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">olimpíjskij <b>surók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Olympic marmot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:седой.html>седо́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sedój <b>surók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">hoary marmot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:серый.html>се́рый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">séryj <b>surók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">gray marmot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:алтайский.html>алта́йский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">altájskij <b>surók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">Altai marmot</span></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">тарбаган</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tarbagan</i> ― <span class="e-translation">tarbagan, tarvaga</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">чёрношапочный <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:камчатский.html>камча́тский</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:восточный.html>восто́чный</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сурок.html>суро́к</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">čórnošapočnyj <b>surók</b>, kamčátskij <b>surók</b>, vostóčnyj <b>surók</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">black-capped marmot</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:суслик.html>су́слик</a> (18686)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сусолу</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">susolu</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, probably onomatopoeic of its calls; related to <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">съскам</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sǎskam</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I hiss</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">свистати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">svistati</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to whistle</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">су-</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">su-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + *тъка (related to  <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тыкать.html>ты́кать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">týkatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>), resulting in <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стык.html>стык</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дня</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>но́чи</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">styk dnja i nóči</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">union of day and night</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сутки.html>су́тки</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">za <b>sútki</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">during the day/ for the day, during 24 hours / for 24 hours</span></div>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:менее.html>ме́нее</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:чем.html>чем</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сутки.html>су́тки</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">méneje, čem za <b>sútki</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">less than 24 hours</span></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сутолока.html>су́толока</a> (23821)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толочь.html>толо́чь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tolóčʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to crush</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:толочься.html>толо́чься</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tolóčʹsja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to crowd, to mill about</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сутолока.html>су́толока</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sútoloka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сутолока.html>су́толоки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сутолока.html>су́толоки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сутолока.html>су́толок</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> hustle and bustle, commotion</li></ol>

***суть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>суть</a> (1570)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>суть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sutʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суть.html>су́ти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суть.html>су́ти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суть.html>су́тей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>essence, core, gist, main point
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1956</b>,  Boris Pasternak,  “Во <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеться.html>хо́чется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дойти.html>дойти́</a> ...”, in  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>Когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:разгуляться.html>разгуля́ется</a></cite>  | <cite>When the Weather Clears</cite> | , published 1960:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:во.html>Во</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всём</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хотеться.html>хо́чется</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дойти.html>дойти́</a> / <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>До</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мой</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:суть.html>су́ти</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vo vsjóm mne xóčetsja dojtí / Do sámoj <b>súti</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">In everything, I want to reach / For the very <b>essence</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сухарь.html>суха́рь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">suxárʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сухарь.html>сухаря́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сухарь.html>сухари́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сухарь.html>сухаре́й</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> countable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a slice or piece of bread, dried or toasted until hard and crisp</li>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dried-up man, a dry old stick; a boring person</li></ol>

***суховатый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:суховатый.html>сухова́тый</a> (24878)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сухой.html>сухо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">suxój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́тый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суховатый.html>сухова́тый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">suxovátyj</span>)
</p>

***сухой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сухой.html>сухо́й</a> (965)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*suxъ</i>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">sohr</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">αὖος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aûos</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latvian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Latvian language">Latvian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lv">sauss</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lithuanian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Lithuanian language">Lithuanian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lt">saũsas</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Persian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Persian language">Persian</a></span> <i class="fa-Arab mention" lang="fa">خشک‎</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="fa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xošk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sanskrit" class="extiw" title="w:Sanskrit">Sanskrit</a></span> <i class="Deva mention" lang="sa">शुष्क</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="sa-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">śuṣka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сухой.html>сухо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">suxój</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:суша.html>су́ше</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сухой.html>сухо́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dry</li>
<li>lean</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> land</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> cool, cold</li>
<li>boring, dull</li></ol>

***сучить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сучить.html>сучи́ть</a> (21700)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сучить.html>сучи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sučítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to spin, to twist, to throw</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to jerk, to work
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сучить.html>сучи́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ножка.html>но́жками</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнке</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sučítʹ</b> nóžkami (o rebjónke)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to kick</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сучок.html>сучок</a> (8109)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сучок.html>сучо́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sučók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сучок.html>сучка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сучок.html>сучки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сучок.html>сучко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>small bough, small branch</li>
<li>knot (whorl in wood left by a branch)</li></ol>

***сушить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сушить.html>суши́ть</a> (12473)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sušìti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сушить.html>суши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sušítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:высушить.html>вы́сушить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dry</li>
<li>to roast, to toast, to parch</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wear out, to exhaust, to torment</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to harden <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">one's heart</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to make heartless</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сушиться.html>суши́ться</a> (15808)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сушить.html>суши́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sušítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сушиться.html>суши́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sušítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́сушиться</b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to dry</li>
